Initializing liblinphone.

\subsubsection{L\+C\+\_\+\+S\+I\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+D\+O\+N\+T\+B\+I\+ND}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define L\+C\+\_\+\+S\+I\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+D\+O\+N\+T\+B\+I\+ND~(-\/2)}



Don\textquotesingle{}t create any server socket for this transport, ie don\textquotesingle{}t bind on any port. 

Use with \#\+Linphone\+Sip\+Transports

\subsubsection{Linphone\+Core\+Auth\+Info\+Requested\+Cb}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef void($\ast$ Linphone\+Core\+Auth\+Info\+Requested\+Cb) (\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$lc, const char $\ast$realm, const char $\ast$username, const char $\ast$domain)}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & the Linphone\+Core \\
\hline

\hline
{\em username} & the username that needs to be authenticated. \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!Linphone\+Core\+Cbs@{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}}
\index{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs@{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \+\_\+\+Linphone\+Core\+Cbs \textbf{ Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}}



That class holds all the callbacks which are called by \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a}. 

Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+core\+\_\+cbs()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga216de83e5bfcf8487d4c22dfc7fcbeb1} to create an instance. Then, call the callback setters on the events you need to monitor and pass the object to a \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} instance through \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga9e29656841fa0026599900a7ec44e53c}.

That class is inherited from belle\+\_\+sip\+\_\+object\+\_\+t. \mbox{\label{group__initializing_gadc0b52beed93a03601943a46712a02c7}}

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!Linphone\+Core\+File\+Transfer\+Recv\+Cb@{Linphone\+Core\+File\+Transfer\+Recv\+Cb}}

\subsubsection{Linphone\+Core\+File\+Transfer\+Recv\+Cb}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef void($\ast$ Linphone\+Core\+File\+Transfer\+Recv\+Cb) (\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$lc, \textbf{ Linphone\+Chat\+Message} $\ast$message, const \textbf{ Linphone\+Content} $\ast$content, const char $\ast$buff, size\+\_\+t size)}



File transfer receive callback prototype. 

This function is called by the core upon an incoming File transfer is started. This function may be call several time for the same file in case of large file. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} object \\
\hline
{\em message} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Chat\+Message}{p.}{group__chatroom_gada79c4417919389b5247e254279f7833} message from which the body is received. \\
\hline
{\em content} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Content}{p.}{group__misc_gaec435ed53168e70535e64b69a906304b} incoming content information \\
\hline
{\em buff} & pointer to the received data \\
\hline
{\em size} & number of bytes to be read from buff. 0 means end of file. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

File transfer send callback prototype. 

This function is called by the core upon an outgoing file transfer is started. This function is called until size is set to 0.

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core\+Cbs} $\ast$}]{cbs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a listener in order to be notified of \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} events. 

Once an event is received, registred \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa4a52a9cdc319baccd2232dda6681f8f} are invoked sequencially. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & The \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} object to monitor. \\
\hline
{\em cbs} & A \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa4a52a9cdc319baccd2232dda6681f8f} object holding the callbacks you need. A reference is taken by \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} until you invoke \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+callbacks()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga60223f605f50ba4a60ca3086240c6369}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\label{group__initializing_gaed2c60f671ebf838e8994013d9fe3400}} 
\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+listener (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table} $\ast$}]{vtable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



add a listener to be notified of linphone core events. 

Once events are received, registered vtable are invoked in order. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em vtable} & a Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table structure holding your application callbacks. Object is owned by linphone core until linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+listener. \\
\hline
{\em lc} & object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\label{group__initializing_ga7bdac8ac386483fc4e0876e4c5d13755}} 
\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Main loop function. 

It is crucial that your application call it periodically.

\doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga7bdac8ac386483fc4e0876e4c5d13755} performs various backgrounds tasks\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item receiving of S\+IP messages
\item handles timers and timeout
\item performs registration to proxies
\item authentication retries The application M\+U\+ST call this function periodically, in its main loop. Be careful that this function must be called from the same thread as other liblinphone methods. If it is not the case make sure all liblinphone calls are serialized with a mutex. For I\+CE to work properly it should be called every 20ms. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\label{group__initializing_ga94b98d58cc47f138bade99749f4db6f2}}

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+migrate\+\_\+to\+\_\+multi\+\_\+transport (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Migrate configuration so that all S\+IP transports are enabled. 

Versions of linphone $<$ 3.\+7 did not support using multiple S\+IP transport simultaneously. This function helps application to migrate the configuration so that all transports are enabled. Existing proxy configuration are added a transport parameter so that they continue using the unique transport that was set previously. This function must be used just after creating the core, before any call to \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga7bdac8ac386483fc4e0876e4c5d13755} 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & the linphone core \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if migration was done, 0 if not done because unnecessary or already done, -\/1 in case of error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__initializing_ga9601ae3c81a1bbf110e84a1a484f3fee}} 
\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Core}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table} $\ast$}]{vtable,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{config\+\_\+path,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{factory\+\_\+config\+\_\+path,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{userdata }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Instanciates a Linphone\+Core object. 

The Linphone\+Core object is the primary handle for doing all phone actions. It should be unique within your application. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em vtable} & a Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table structure holding your application callbacks \\
\hline
{\em config\+\_\+path} & a path to a config file. If it does not exists it will be created. The config file is used to store all settings, call logs, friends, proxies... so that all these settings become persistent over the life of the Linphone\+Core object. It is allowed to set a N\+U\+LL config file. In that case Linphone\+Core will not store any settings. \\
\hline
{\em factory\+\_\+config\+\_\+path} & a path to a read-\/only config file that can be used to to store hard-\/coded preference such as proxy settings or internal preferences. The settings in this factory file always override the one in the normal config file. It is O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL, use N\+U\+LL if unneeded. \\
\hline
{\em userdata} & an opaque user pointer that can be retrieved at any time (for example in callbacks) using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+user\+\_\+data()}{p.}{group__initializing_gadd8c0eeb93eadb513d94549898c339d1}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new\+\_\+with\+\_\+config}{p.}{group__initializing_gab3739459d3d102f97f5a0b2106fac6ea} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+core()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga0f71be9d7c8fac862e2f929ed0419e80} instead.  \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+log\+\_\+level\+\_\+mask()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+log\+\_\+level\+\_\+mask (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{loglevel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Define the log level using mask. 

The loglevel parameter is a bitmask parameter. Therefore to enable only warning and error messages, use O\+R\+T\+P\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG $\vert$ O\+R\+T\+P\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR. To disable logs, simply set loglevel to 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em loglevel} & A bitmask of the log levels to set. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Set the maximum number of simultaneous calls Linphone core can manage at a time. 

All new call above this limit are declined with a busy answer 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+provisioning\+\_\+uri (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{uri }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set U\+RI where to download xml configuration file at startup. 

This can also be set from configuration file or factory config file, from [misc] section, item \char`\"{}config-\/uri\char`\"{}. Calling this function does not load the configuration. It will write the value into configuration so that configuration from remote U\+RI will take place at next Linphone\+Core start. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & the linphone core \\
\hline
{\em uri} & the http or https uri to use in order to download the configuration. Passing N\+U\+LL will disable remote provisioning. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if uri could not be parsed, 0 otherwise. Note that this does not check validity of U\+RI endpoint nor scheme and download may still fail. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__initializing_ga24c7276e70ba9a1cccd1c55c1e15499b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+clean (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Clean the factory. 

This function is generally useless as the factory is unique per process, however calling this function at the end avoid getting reports from belle-\/sip leak detector about memory leaked in \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+get()}{p.}{group__initializing_gad5c6ec08691a00b9c3225b774fe1dc68}. \mbox{\label{group__initializing_ga15d1de56e0ec023c766b90f4b283c86f}}

\index{Initializing@{Initializing}!linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info@{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info@{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info}!Initializing@{Initializing}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Auth\+Info}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Factory} $\ast$}]{factory,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{username,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{userid,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{passwd,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{ha1,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{realm,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{domain }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a \doxyref{Linphone\+Auth\+Info}{p.}{group__authentication_ga0f8289c1aab407992864a68869107f4f} object. 

The object can be created empty, that is with all arguments set to N\+U\+LL. Username, userid, password, realm and domain can be set later using specific methods. At the end, username and passwd (or ha1) are required. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em factory} & The \doxyref{Linphone\+Factory}{p.}{group__initializing_ga3ce8cc4b9af4382f08540edc368f7310} singleton. \\
\hline
{\em username} & The username that needs to be authenticated \\
\hline
{\em userid} & The userid used for authenticating (use N\+U\+LL if you don\textquotesingle{}t know what it is) \\
\hline
{\em passwd} & The password in clear text \\
\hline
{\em ha1} & The ha1-\/encrypted password if password is not given in clear text. \\
\hline
{\em realm} & The authentication domain (which can be larger than the sip domain. Unfortunately many S\+IP servers don\textquotesingle{}t use this parameter. \\
\hline
{\em domain} & The S\+IP domain for which this authentication information is valid, if it has to be restricted for a single S\+IP domain. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A \doxyref{Linphone\+Auth\+Info}{p.}{group__authentication_ga0f8289c1aab407992864a68869107f4f} object. linphone\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info\+\_\+destroy() must be used to destroy it when no longer needed. The Linphone\+Core makes a copy of Linphone\+Auth\+Info passed through \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+auth\+\_\+info()}{p.}{group__authentication_ga62ac5bb34f0342f7edc733c42473b7aa}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__initializing_gab6e69c9eae9550424929a48bb8570015}}

Instanciate a \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} object. 

The Linphone\+Core object is the primary handle for doing all phone actions. It should be unique within your application. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em factory} & The \doxyref{Linphone\+Factory}{p.}{group__initializing_ga3ce8cc4b9af4382f08540edc368f7310} singleton. \\
\hline
{\em cbs} & a \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa4a52a9cdc319baccd2232dda6681f8f} object holding your application callbacks. A reference will be taken on it until the destruciton of the core or the unregistration with linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+cbs(). \\
\hline
{\em config\+\_\+path} & a path to a config file. If it does not exists it will be created. The config file is used to store all settings, call logs, friends, proxies... so that all these settings become persistent over the life of the Linphone\+Core object. It is allowed to set a N\+U\+LL config file. In that case Linphone\+Core will not store any settings. \\
\hline
{\em factory\+\_\+config\+\_\+path} & a path to a read-\/only config file that can be used to to store hard-\/coded preference such as proxy settings or internal preferences. The settings in this factory file always override the one in the normal config file. It is O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL, use N\+U\+LL if unneeded. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+new\+\_\+with\+\_\+config}{p.}{group__initializing_gab3739459d3d102f97f5a0b2106fac6ea} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Instantiates a Linphone\+Core object with a given Lp\+Config. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em factory} & The \doxyref{Linphone\+Factory}{p.}{group__initializing_ga3ce8cc4b9af4382f08540edc368f7310} singleton. The Linphone\+Core object is the primary handle for doing all phone actions. It should be unique within your application. \\
\hline
{\em cbs} & a \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+Cbs}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa4a52a9cdc319baccd2232dda6681f8f} object holding your application callbacks. A reference will be taken on it until the destruciton of the core or the unregistration with linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+cbs(). \\
\hline
{\em config} & a pointer to an Lp\+Config object holding the configuration of the Linphone\+Core to be instantiated. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
